x20\40\x20\x20\x20\x20\40\x66\x6f\x6e\164\x2d\163\164\171\x6c\x65\x3a\x20\151\x74\x61\154\151\143\xa\40\40\40\40\x20\40\x20\x20\175\xa\xa\40\40\x20\x20\x20\40\x20\x20\x2e\142\164\156\x2d\x73\x75\142\155\x69\x74\40\173\12\40\x20\x20\x20\x20\x20\x20\40\x20\40\40\40\160\x61\144\144\x69\156\147\72\x20\67\x70\x78\x20\x32\65\160\170\73\12\40\40\40\40\x20\40\40\40\40\40\x20\40\x62\x6f\x72\x64\145\x72\72\x20\x32\160\170\40\163\157\154\151\x64\x20\147\x72\145\171\x3b\xa\40\40\x20\x20\x20\x20\40\40\40\40\x20\x20\x62\157\162\144\145\x72\55\162\141\x64\151\165\163\x3a\x20\x34\x70\170\12\40\x20\x20\40\40\40\x20\40\175\12\xa\40\40\x20\x20\40\40\x20\40\x2e\x66\x6f\162\x6d\55\146\151\x6c\145\54\12\40\x20\x20\40\40\40\40\x20\x61\72\x68\x6f\166\x65\x72\x20\x7b\12\40\40\x20\x20\40\40\x20\40\x20\40\x20\x20\143\x6f\x6c\x6f\x72\72\x20\43\143\x35\x63\x38\x64\x36\xa\40\40\x20\x20\40\40\x20\40\175\xa\xa\x20\x20\40\40\40\x20\x20\x20\x2e\x62\x74\x6e\55\x73\165\142\155\151\x74\x3a\x68\x6f\x76\145\162\x20\173\xa\40\x20\40\x20\40\x20\40\x20\x20\40\x20\40\142\x6f\x72\144\x65\162\x3a\40\62\x70\170\40\163\x6f\154\x69\144\40\43\x63\65\143\x38\x64\66\12\x20\40\40\40\x20\x20\40\x20\175\12\xa\40\x20\x20\40\x20\40\x20\x20\56\146\x6f\162\x6d\x2d\x75\x70\x6c\x6f\x61\x64\x20\x7b\xa\40\x20\40\x20\40\x20\40\40\40\40\40\x20\x6d\x61\x72\x67\x69\156\x3a\x20\61\60\x70\170\40\60\xa\x20\40\x20\x20\x20\x20\40\40\x7d\xa\12\40\40\x20\40\x20\40\x20\40\x2e\146\157\x72\155\55\146\151\x6c\145\x20\x7b\xa\40\x20\40\40\x20\40\40\40\40\x20\40\x20\142\157\162\x64\x65\x72\x3a\40\62\x70\x78\x20\163\x6f\x6c\151\144\40\147\x72\145\171\73\12\x20\40\40\40\x20\40\x20\x20\x20\x20\x20\x20\x70\x61\144\144\x69\156\147\72\40\x37\160\170\40\62\x30\x70\x78\73\xa\x20\40\x20\40\x20\x20\x20\x20\40\40\40\x20\x62\157\162\144\x65\x72\x2d\162\141\144\151\165\x73\x3a\x20\64\160\x78\12\x20\x20\40\40\x20\40\40\40\175\12\12\x20\x20\40\x20\x20\x20\40\x20\56\x6d\x65\156\165\55\x74\157\157\x6c\163\x20\173\xa\40\x20\x20\40\x20\40\40\x20\40\40\40\x20\167\
